# Appendix

## Personnel Information Field Distinction Table

| Field Name | Meaning | Type | Example |
| :------------------------------------- | :------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | :----------- | :------------------------------------ |
| Commissioner of data set | The initiator or sponsor of the data collection work | Recommended, multiple selection possible | Company A |
| Data set generator / modeler | The executor specifically responsible for data creation | Recommended, multiple selection possible | Research Institute B, Team C |
| Data entry by | The person specifically responsible for data entry | Optional, single selection | Person D |
| Registration authority | Data supervision/registration authority | Optional, single selection | IEDA |
| Owner of data set | The person who owns the intellectual property rights of the data (may be different from the commissioner) | Recommended, single selection | Company A |
| Entities or persons with exclusive access to this data set | The person who has absolute access to the dataset | Optional, multiple selection | Group E |

## Flow Classification Dataset

### Basic Flow Classification

| **Category ID** | **Classification Name**         | Remarks                                                                     |
| --------------- | -------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **1**           | **Emissions**                    |                                                                              |
| 1.1             | Emissions to water bodies        |                                                                              |
| 1.1.1           | Emissions to freshwater          |                                                                              |
| 1.1.2           | Emissions to seawater            |                                                                              |
| 1.1.3           | Emissions to water, unspecified  |                                                                              |
| 1.1.4           | Emissions to water, unspecified (long-term) | Refers to emissions occurring within the next 100 years                     |
| 1.2             | Emissions to soil                |                                                                              |
| 1.2.1           | Emissions to agricultural soil   |                                                                              |
| 1.2.2           | Emissions to non-agricultural soil |                                                                              |
| 1.2.3           | Emissions to soil, unspecified   |                                                                              |
| 1.2.4           | Emissions to soil, unspecified (long-term) | Refers to emissions occurring within the next 100 years                     |
| 1.3             | Emissions to atmosphere          |                                                                              |
| 1.3.1           | Emissions to urban near-ground atmosphere | Refers to emissions within 40 meters above ground level                     |
| 1.3.2           | Emissions to non-urban atmosphere or from tall stacks | Refers to emissions above 40 meters above ground level                     |
| 1.3.3           | Emissions to low stratosphere and high troposphere | e.g., emissions from aircraft combustion engines                           |
| 1.3.4           | Emissions to atmosphere, unspecified |                                                                              |
| 1.3.5           | Emissions to atmosphere, unspecified (long-term) | Refers to emissions occurring within the next 100 years                     |
| **2**           | **Resources**                    |                                                                              |
| 2.1             | Terrestrial resources            |                                                                              |
| 2.1.1           | Non-renewable terrestrial material resources | e.g., "sand," "anhydrite; 100%"                                           |
| 2.1.2           | Non-renewable terrestrial elemental resources | e.g., "gold," "copper"                                                   |
| 2.1.3           | Non-renewable terrestrial energy resources | e.g., "hard coal; 32.7 MJ/kg net calorific value," "uranium; natural isotope mix; 451000 MJ/kg" |
| 2.1.4           | Renewable terrestrial elemental resources | e.g., "radon"                                                             |
| 2.1.5           | Renewable terrestrial energy resources | e.g., "wind energy," "hydropower; run-of-river"                           |
| 2.1.6           | Renewable terrestrial material resources |                                                                              |
| 2.1.7           | Renewable terrestrial resources, unspecified | Refers to basic flows of renewable terrestrial resources not fitting other categories |
| 2.1.8           | Non-renewable terrestrial resources, unspecified | Refers to basic flows of non-renewable terrestrial resources not fitting other categories |
| 2.2             | Water body resources             |                                                                              |
| 2.2.1           | Non-renewable water material resources | e.g., magnesium, bromine, hydrogen                                        |
| 2.2.2           | Non-renewable water elemental resources |                                                                              |
| 2.2.3           | Non-renewable water energy resources |                                                                              |
| 2.2.4           | Renewable water elemental resources |                                                                              |
| 2.2.5           | Renewable water energy resources |                                                                              |
| 2.2.6           | Renewable water material resources |                                                                              |
| 2.2.7           | Renewable water resources, unspecified |                                                                              |
| 2.2.8           | Non-renewable water resources, unspecified |                                                                              |
| 2.3             | Atmospheric resources            |                                                                              |
| 2.3.1           | Non-renewable atmospheric material resources |                                                                              |
| 2.3.2           | Non-renewable atmospheric elemental resources |                                                                              |
| 2.3.3           | Non-renewable atmospheric energy resources |                                                                              |
| 2.3.4           | Renewable atmospheric elemental resources | e.g., "oxygen," "argon"                                                  |
| 2.3.5           | Renewable atmospheric energy resources | e.g., wind energy, solar energy                                          |
| 2.3.6           | Renewable atmospheric material resources |                                                                              |
| 2.3.7           | Renewable atmospheric resources, unspecified | Refers to basic flows of renewable atmospheric resources not fitting other categories |
| 2.3.8           | Non-renewable atmospheric resources, unspecified | Refers to basic flows of non-renewable atmospheric resources not fitting other categories |
| 2.4             | Biosphere resources              |                                                                              |
| 2.4.1           | Renewable biosphere elemental resources | For extraction/hunting of wild species, e.g., "teak (Tectona grandis), bark-free; standing timber; primary forest" |
| 2.4.2           | Renewable biosphere energy resources | e.g., "roundwood cork; 50% moisture"                                      |
| 2.4.3           | Renewable biosphere material resources | e.g., "wood biomass; 50% moisture, 7.2 MJ/kg"                             |
| 2.4.4           | Renewable biosphere genetic resources |                                                                              |
| 2.4.5           | Renewable biosphere resources, unspecified | Refers to basic flows of renewable biosphere resources not fitting other categories |
| **3**           | **Land Use**                     |                                                                              |
| 3.1             | Land use                         |                                                                              |
| 3.2             | Land transformation              |                                                                              |
| **4**           | **Other Basic Flows**            |                                                                              |
